NewsPublicationsDownloadsCoursesContactİAdminLiu Zhi <name>־</name><title>Professor </title>School of Communication and Information Engineering, Shanghai University, China PO Box 83, Shanghai University, No. 99 ShangDa Road,Shanghai 200444, China Email:Biography<edu>Zhi Liu received the B.E. and M.E. degrees from Tianjin University, Tianjin, China, and the Ph.D. degree from Institute of Image Processing and Pattern Recognition, Shanghai Jiaotong University, Shanghai, China, in 1999, 2002, and 2005, respectively </edu>. He is currently a Professor with the <aff>School of Communication and Information Engineering, Shanghai University </aff>, Shanghai, China. From Aug. 2012 to Aug. 2014, he was a Visiting Researcher with the SIROCCO Team, IRISA/INRIA-Rennes, France, with the support by EU FP7 Marie Curie Actions. He has published more than 150 refereed technical papers in international journals and conferences. <domain>His research interests include image/video processing, machine learning, computer vision and multimedia communication </domain>. <aocial>He was a TPC member/session chair in ICIP 2017, PCM 2016, VCIP 2016, ICME 2014, WIAMIS 2013, etc. He co-organized special sessions on visual attention, saliency models, and applications at WIAMIS 2013 and ICME 2014. He is an area editor of Signal Processing: Image Communication and served as a guest editor for the special issue on Recent Advances in Saliency Models, Applications and Evaluations in Signal Processing: Image Communication. He is a senior member of IEEE. </aocial>More papersȨ  Ϻѧ ICP09014157ַϺбɽϴ·99ţܱ߽ͨ  ʱࣺ200444 绰ѯ֧֣ϺѧϢ칫Ҡ He became a researcher in postdoctoral station of civil engineering in HIT in May 2008 and began to work in June of the same year. Doctor Xin has been teaching Bridge Wind Engineering, and his research fields are focused on wind-induced vibration theoryof long-span bridges and high-rise buildings, and flow control for wind-induced actions on structures, and wind-rain two-phase flow and its actions on structures, and aerodynamic performance optimization of fan blades, and so on. He has been taking charge oftwo project from National Natural Science Foundation, andtwo sub-project from state science and technology support program, and also he has been chairing or participating in some other research projects. About 40 papers have been published in journals or conferences, includingmanyof SCI indexed, or EI indexed, or ISTP indexed. He has obtained fiveinvention patents, and he has supervised seven undergraduates, andten postgraduates, and two Ph.
